 vimaanan company ne spasht kiya ki 90 minute se kam kii udaan main pehle bhi shaakaahaari khaanaa miltaa tha
 As all the rules are the same, it has been decided to serve hot vegetarian food instead of only cold vegetarian snacks
 air india ne shanivaar ko jari ek bayaan main kaha, '60 se 90 minute kii gharelu udaan kii iconomi class main ab garm shaakaahaari khaanaa milegaa
 This rule will be implemented from January 1, 2016
 'tippaniyan After this decision of Air India, there was a debate all over the country and many people criticized this decision
 air india ne saath hi kaha, 'yatriyon kii pratikriya ke baad isaki samiksha kii jaaegi

 ' The airline made it clear that earlier in less than 90 minutes flight, vegetarian food was available

 The High Court has canceled the acquisition of 127 farmers' land acquired for Naya Raipur on Tuesday
 court ne kaha ki bhoomi adhigrahan kanoon kii dhajjiyaan udaakar afasarone kisaanon kii jameenon par kabja kiya tha
 Naya Raipur in Chhattisgarh made a lot of headlines for being the new capital of the state
 nayaa raipur ab atal nagar ke naam se janaa jane laga he, lekin atal nagar ke vikaas ke naam par kuch kisaanon kii jameen jabaran hadap lee gai
 These farmers neither received quadruple compensation of their agricultural land nor did the government fix a reasonable price for their land
 aakhirkaar kisaanon ne apni jameen waapas paane ke liye adaalat kaa darwaja khatkhataya
 After hearing for several months, the High Court has canceled the process of acquiring the land of 127 farmers after finally not complying with the provisions of the Land Acquisition Act
 bilaspur hoicourt ke is faisle ke baad peedit kisaanon ne raahat kii saans lee he
 After hearing a petition challenging the process of land acquisition of the suffering farmers of Atal Nagar, Justice Prashant Mishra's bench has directed the state government to complete the process again as per the rules
 nayaa raipur ke vikaas ke liye NRDA ne 21 march 2013 ko 128
 a notification for acquisition of 39 acres of land was issued
 iske tahat raipur ke aarang ke rico gaanv main rahane vaale kai kisaanon kii jameen adhigrahit karne kaa farmaan sunaaya gaya tha
 After the government notification, the NRDA started the process of acquiring land of 125 farmers including Kuldeep, Lakeshwar Prasad
 is bich 1 janvari 2014 se jameen adhigrahan ke liye bhberjan main paardarshita or uchit muaavje kaa adhikaar adhinium 2013 lagu ho gaya
 The farmers had filed a petition in the High Court in 2016, seeking to cancel the entire process of land acquisition and compensation as per the provisions of the old Act
 yachikakartaon kii daleel thi ki nae adhinium ke tahat 12 maah ke bheetar muaavje kii raashi unhen mil jaani chahie thi
 Under the old Act also compensation should have been given before 3 January 2015, but this was not done in his case
 NRDA ne tamaam niyamon kaa ulanghan karte hue sthaneey graminon kii jameen apane kabje main le lee
 After hearing the arguments of the petitioner and the government side, the High Court has said in its order that due to non-compliance of the provisions prescribed in land acquisition cases, the process of land acquisition is not lawful
 lihaaja use nirast kiya jaataa he
 The court, in its directive, has given exemption to the state government that if necessary in the interest of the common people, a fresh process can be started by following the rules set for land acquisition

 sutron ke mutabik iskar vibhaag ne fori taur par wo sari benami sampatti jabt kar lee he jo lalu yadav ke bacchon se judi hui bataai jaati he
 Orders have been issued today to confiscate the benami property related to Lalu's children
 lalu yadav kii badi beti or rajyasabha kii saansad misa bharti ko iskar vibhaag ne talab kiya he
 He has been asked to come to the Income Tax Department office in the first week of July to clarify on benami transactions
 isse pehle iskar vibhaag ne 50 karod kii sampatti jabt kii thi
 According to the Benami Act, the department has to give 90 days time to clarify
 agarsambandhit pakshaisamen vifal rahata he to jabti or kurki kii karrwai kii jaati he
 It is noteworthy that the Income Tax Department sent summons to Misa Bharti and her husband Shailesh Kumar twice but they did not appear
 unke vakil ne iske peeche media or suraksha kaarnon ko vajah bataaya
 Earlier, the Income Tax Department also imposed a fine of Rs 10,000 on Misa Bharti for not appearing on June 6

 In view of the possibility of terrorist attack in Delhi on Independence Day, Delhi has been kept on high alert
 jaankaree ke mutabik tamaam railway stesan, metro stesan or bheed-bhaad vaali jagahon par suraksha vyavastha kaaphi sakht kar di gai he
 a security review has been done at this link at the New Delhi Railway Station
 railway stesan ke entry point par RPF or dilli railway police ne joint oparation ke tahat checking kii
 Every vehicle and person was searched extensively with the help of a bomb squad besides a dog squad
 iske alaava stesan par kaam karne kuliyon ko bhi jaagruk kiya gaya
 Police say that the coolie stays at the station overnight
 thodi jaagrukta kii vajah se ye police kii aankh or kaan sabit ho sakate hai
 In the last phase of the security review, police took stock of security on the platform
 ek-ek saamaan ko khoji kutton kii madad se check kiya gaya
 Apart from this, the police team was also seen patrolling inside the train
 suraksha agenciyon ne chetaya he ki aatanki har haal main apane napak mansoobon ko kaamyaab karne kii koshish karenge
 In such a situation, Delhi Police is also claiming all preparations
 police ne saaf taur par kaha he ki dillivaasiyon kisi baat kii phikr karne kii zarurat nahin he
 Celebrations of freedom will not be allowed to disturb any kind
 bataa den ki dilli police ko mili alert main kaha gaya he ki 15 agast ke maukey par 2 alag lokation par aatanki hamalaa kar sakate hai
 Therefore, the Delhi Police has been ordered to remain on high alert, the alert said that the police especially keep a special watch on the bus stand, famous temple, dargah, church, airport, government building and offices

 ' In his editorial titled 'geeta Sage Farewell', The Nation described Geeta wandering off to Pakistan, living under the Edi Foundation here in Karachi and then back to India
 akhbaar ne likhaa he ki gita kii dekhbhaal ke prati apni kritagyata jataane ke liye bharat ke pradhanmantri narendra modi ne idi foundation ko ek karod rupee dene kaa elaan kiya

" yah pakistan ke suraksha sanchaalkon ke liye raahat banakar aayaa hoga ki idi foundation ne paisa nahin liya, nahin to ek or badi bahes shuru ho jaati jo vichaaron ko bharat banaam pakistan ke naam par or baant detii
